						<h2 class="post-box-title"><a href="https://blogchiasekienthuc.com/marketing/ma-giam-gia-gpm-login.html" rel="bookmark">Mã giảm giá GPMLogin (-150.000đ trên tổng đơn)</a></h2>
						<p class="post-meta">
	
<span class="tie-date"><i class="fa fa-clock-o"></i>24/02/2025</span>	
	<span class="post-comments"><i class="fa fa-comments"></i><a href="https://blogchiasekienthuc.com/marketing/ma-giam-gia-gpm-login.html#respond">0</a></span>

													<div class="post-thumbnail">
							<a href="https://blogchiasekienthuc.com/marketing/ma-giam-gia-gpm-login.html" rel="bookmark">
								<img width="310" height="141" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20310%20141'%3E%3C/svg%3E" class="attachment-tie-medium size-tie-medium wp-post-image" alt="gpm-login-voucher" decoding="async" data-lazy-src="https://blogchiasekienthuc.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/02/gpm-login-voucher.png" /><noscript><img width="310" height="141" src="https://blogchiasekienthuc.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/02/gpm-login-voucher.png" class="attachment-tie-medium size-tie-medium wp-post-image" alt="gpm-login-voucher" decoding="async" /></noscript>								<span class="fa overlay-icon"></span>
							</a>
						</div><!-- post-thumbnail /-->
							
						<div class="entry">
							<p>Vâng, nếu bạn làm trong lĩnh vực MMO (kiếm tiền online), đặc biệt là trong lĩnh vực bán tài khoản/phần mềm thì bạn sẽ biết đến phần mềm GPMLogin đúng không ạ. <script>
    /* check if there is a div with chest id in the post */
    var check_chest = document.getElementById("chest");
    if (check_chest) {
          /* get the chest content */
        var chest_content = check_chest.innerHTML; 
         /* get the content title and show it on the locker to intrigue user to share */
        var content_hint = jQuery('#chest .content-hint')[0].innerHTML;
         /* get the lock content */
        var lock_content = '<div id="lock"><div class="lock_content"><p class="locker-title"><i class="fa fa-lock"></i> NỘI DUNG BÍ MẬT <i class="fa fa-lock"></i></p><p class="content-hint" style="">'+content_hint+'</p><div class="fb-like" data-href="'+location.href+'" data-layout="button_count" data-action="like" data-size="large" data-show-faces="true" data-share="true"></div><br /><br /><p>Bạn vui lòng chờ trong <strong id="countbox"></strong> để xem nội dung ẩn. Like và <strong><i class="fa fa-facebook-square"></i> share</strong> nếu bạn thích bài viết này nha!</p><p class="unlock-now"><i class="fa fa-key"></i> CHỜ TÝ NHÉ :) <i class="fa fa-key"></i></p></div></div>';
      
        /* countdown function */
        function countchest(wait) {
            var timeleft = wait;
            var downloadTimer = setInterval(function() {
                document.getElementById("countbox").innerHTML = timeleft + " seconds";
                timeleft -= 1;
                if (timeleft <= 0) {
                    clearInterval(downloadTimer);
                    document.getElementById("countbox").innerHTML = "";
                    jQuery('#chest').html(chest_content);
                }
            }, 1000);
        }

        /* start the countdown - you can replace 1800 with any amount of seconds you like */
        
        /* get the chest unique series */
        var chest_seri = jQuery('#chest')[0].getAttribute('data-seri');
        /* update: show the content if shared */
        if (localStorage.getItem(chest_seri) != null) {
               jQuery('#chest').html(chest_content);
        } else {
               /* replace chest content */
               jQuery('#chest').html(lock_content);
               countchest(10);
               /* when I user click on locker, open the dialog for sharing */
        }  
    }
</script>
<script>
/* loading facebook sdk */
(function(d, s, id) {
    var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
    if (d.getElementById(id)) return;
    js = d.createElement(s);
    js.id = id;
    js.src = 'https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/sdk.js#xfbml=1&version=v3.1&appId=1594797160531594&autoLogAppEvents=1';
    fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
}(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));
</script>
